| <span data-ttu-id="9efff-824">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9efff-824">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9efff-825">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9efff-825">Value</span></span> |
